# Text Elements
Acid + Alkali Experiments ^5fGz1XOq

-> Your solution is colorless - No
indication if it is finished
-> They dissolve easily ^fnmb8J5Y

To check pH of sol ^3w4NuLjo

Checked when color changed ^vMnDcRCk

Indicator is 
still an impurity! ^giONmoCA

Charcoal is capable of Absorbing
the indicator and since it is INSOLUBLE
it can be filted ^2aqizpAS

Filter ^dsYkhTlP

Aqueous NaCl ^dEdKfj8h

Evaropation ^zKlhnc2N

Crystallisation ^sGMzQSRr

Solution is heat
Solubility increased ^5uxmaGSs

Solution is cooled
Solubility decreases
Salt Crystals form ^vD2PLtSO
